$sns_description[1] = 'In my world there are many different nations, and they constantly fight for a place under the sun. Innumerable hordes of nomads besiege rich cities surrounded by high walls. Wild tribes inhabit the forests and swamps, earning a living from caravan robberies. Great kings rule with huge empires.'
$sns_description[2] = 'My world is great and immense. I know that to the east lies the endless sea. The far south is inhabited by wild people with skin as black as the night itself. To the north are impenetrable forests in which there live undersized, but evil tribes of hunters. The western steppes are ruled by nomads who live by robbery and destroy cities.'
$sns_description[3] = 'In my world there are many different cultures and nations. There are kings, whose treasuries are full of gold, black magicians, with power above that of even kings, and fearless heroes who are not afraid of even magicians. But there were more, of course, all ordinary people - peasants, soldiers, artisans, and merchants.'

$medieval_description[1] = 'My country has a very beautiful nature: a lot of forests, meadows, rivers, and lakes. The mountains are covered with shiny snowcaps. All those lands are owned by the barons and knights who serve the king and collect tribute from the peasants living near their castles. Ordinary people live a difficult life.'
$medieval_description[2] = 'In my world every man has his place and everyone knows what to do. Kings and barons ruled their lands, knights fights with their enemies, artisans make pots and tools, farmers plow the land, and the priests pray for all of them and help with good advice.'
$medieval_description[3] = 'My world is very big, so I do not know everything about it. People in cities live richly, but it is dirty, crowded, and smells bad. Barons and knights sits in their stone castles or go on military campaigns. And the peasants in the villages plow all year round to feed those and others.'

$darkfantasy_description[1] = 'As I can remember, we always had a hard time. It is said that once upon a time, under the old empire, people lived richly and happily. But now the forests are full of robbers and wild animals, barons can not and do not want to maintain order in their lands, and the peasants under their oppression are starving almost every winter.'
$darkfantasy_description[2] = 'Life in my world is not easy. In the dark forests lurk terrible creatures that can ruin an entire village. Eastern necromancers raise armies of undead, and warlocks rule the western lands, whispering orders to kings. Of course there are heroes who fight back against this evil, but they are too few.'
$darkfantasy_description[3] = 'The priests say that our world is dying, and the end is near. The dead arise from their graves and roam at night through abandoned ancient cities. Dragons burn down villages and devour cattle. The Black Death decimates both children and the elderly. And each following year is worse than the one before.'

$highfantasy_description[1] = 'My world is ruled by powerful archmages which form the Great Conclave and decide the fate of mortals on it. But they do not interfere in ordinary life. Cities thrive, although, of course, wealth entails corruption and theft. And the sorcerers’ experiments sometimes ends with serious troubles.'
$highfantasy_description[2] = 'My world is an arena of war between good and evil. The union of elves, humans, and dwarves from time immemorial oppose the machinations of the King Necromancer who wants to enslave all the free land and populate it with his ugly slaves: goblins, trolls, and dragons.'
$highfantasy_description[3] = 'Our world is very large. I know nothing about the lands beyond the seas, but in my homeland there were seven kingdoms. Now they are united into one great empire. It is said that in the north, behind the Great Wall, an Ancient Evil is waiting in the wings. And when the Long Winter comes, Evil will wake and bring innumerable troubles to the people of the Empire.'

$steampunk_description[1] = 'My world is ruled by science and technology. There are several advanced empires that are vying for influence in the underdeveloped but resource-rich colonies. The advantage will go to the one who has more modern battleships, airships, and steam engines.'
$steampunk_description[2] = 'Science and technology are developed very highly in my world. We use advanced steam engines for transport and industry. To plan production we use powerful arithmometers. For transcontinental flights we have giant zeppelins.'
$steampunk_description[3] = 'In my world there are a few advanced countries where an industrial revolution was achieved. Military and technological power is based on coal and steel. The villages are low on people, because many youth are going to work in the cities. Sometimes it is impossible to breathe from all factory soot, and the fish in the rivers suffocate due to toxic waste.'

$industrial_description[1] = 'Although in my world there are many different states, everyone understands that real power is in the hands of the bankers and industrialists. Working people create trade unions and go on strike, but the government will not tolerate such disturbances and suppresses them very severely. People are angry; many of them live in poverty and cannot find work.'
$industrial_description[2] = 'In my world there was a very big war, it was even called a World War because it involved almost all states. Bombing, artillery shelling, gas attacks - all of it has become habit not only for the soldiers in the trenches, but also for the civilians. There is not enough food, and everything is rationed.'
$industrial_description[3] = 'In my world, a Great War was recently ended. It was so terrible that after the settlement agreement, all the countries in the world united into the World League to prevent its recurrence. Industry is gradually recovering, but there is still a lot of devastation. Sometimes revolutions even occur, and regimes are changed.'

$modern_description[1] = 'In my world there are a lot of different countries, but only some of them are really well-developed and rich. In the others reign poverty and devastation, many of them ruled by dictators. These backward countries - are real hotbeds of terrorism, and the civilized countries sometimes find it necessary to use force.'
$modern_description[2] = 'We have one country that is richer and more powerful than the others. But although everyone tries to be equal to it, there is now a severe crisis, and because of that the economy suffers all over the world. Unemployment is growing, and inflation rising. People all over the world go out to the demonstrations. In many countries civil wars have already started.'
$modern_description[3] = 'Once in my world, there were two great Empires that fought eachother for dominance in the world. But then one of them broke to pieces, and now most of the world adopted the same value system. Most likely, over time, the border between states will disappear and the world will be united.'

$cyberpunk_description[1] = 'My world is ruled by information. Global networks connect the most remote corners of the planet. On the Web you can find everything: movies, music, games, information of any sort, and entertainment. 95% of the population lives on allowances, barely enough for food. But as long as there is entertainment, there are no objections.'
$cyberpunk_description[2] = 'My world is divided into States and Enclaves. Though more people live in states, they are just a dying form of social organization. Enclaves are entirely owned by corporations and obey corporate laws. And it is Enclaves which own wealth and technology.'
$cyberpunk_description[3] = 'My world is ruled by multinational corporations. The state as a form of government does not exist, the laws are written by corporate management, and their one overarching goal - is profit. Those who have money can afford everything. And those who do not... there will always be a place in the shade of society, among scum and synthetic drugs.'

$utopia_description[1] = 'In my world people reached harmony with nature and have forgotten forever about famine, wars, crimes, and diseases. A flexible system of governance involving all the adult population of the planet can quickly solve any problem and fairly distribute resources.'
$utopia_description[2] = 'In our world science and technology have stepped so far ahead that the need for hard work and the competition for resources has disappeared for the individual. Laws are written by outstanding people of culture, and only in poetic form. In the upbringing of children, special attention is paid to the development of aesthetic sense.'
$utopia_description[3] = 'Thanks to social progress we have been able to arrange society so perfectly that the need for states, wars, police, and other instruments of violence has disappeared. All people live in peace and prosperity. Every citizen should draw well and compose poetry. Conflicts are settled only through negotiation.'

$darkfuture_description[1] = 'In my world there is only one decent state. We live by the precepts of the Great Leader and are constantly fighting for freedom and brotherhood. Our enemies are trying to break us and poison us with their propaganda, but we know that only our people live happily and freely. All the necessary rations are distributed equitably.'
$darkfuture_description[2] = 'In my world there are three states, but only in ours do people live organized and happy. Big Brother is always watching over us and helps us not to go astray. The Ministry of Truth explains all unclear questions. Norms on human food are growing steadily, and the war is about to end with our unconditional victory.'
$darkfuture_description[3] = 'I live in a world of justice and equality. We all wear the same uniform, and there is no difference between races and genders. All homes are the same, with transparent walls. We are governed by the Benefactor, who is always elected unanimously. Feelings are under strict medicamental control in order to avoid suffering.'

$space_description[1] = 'The universe contains many inhabited worlds, and we can move freely between them thanks to the hyperdrive. Thousands of planets are combined to form the Galactic Republic, all controlled by the Senate. Of course, each world has their view of life, and conflicts are frequent. The threat of separatism is greater than ever.'
$space_description[2] = 'The universe is much bigger than any one world. Our planet has been united in a global state and has colonized many worlds. But the universe is infinite. We are exploring it, becoming acquainted with alien civilizations, learning, and developing.'

$family_description['orphan'] = 'I do not remember my parents, maybe they died when I was little, or maybe they didn’t care to feed an extra mouth. Overall, my family became the homeless beggars and other waifs. Since childhood I have had to learn to gather food and spend the night on the street.'

My father and brothers worked in the fields or in the woods, and I helped my mother to spin yarn and graze the geese. With the other children we used to play tag and hide-and-seek at the forest’s edge.'
$family_description['gypsy'] = 'I was brought up by gypsies in a traveling encampment who never stayed in one place for more than a few weeks. My life was pretty carefree, though hungry. Wearing whatever came to hand, I would steal and beg for change, but I was free as the wind.'
$family_description['church'] = 'Since infancy, I became an orphan, but I was lucky enough to get into a church shelter. The monks taught us how to behave, help with the housework, and to worship God. The most able of us studied reading and writing. Of course, sometimes we were naughty, and because of that I was often flogged or locked in a cell.'
$family_description['craftsman'] = 'As long as I can remember, I have lived in the city. My father had a pottery and a shop with it. My brothers kneaded clay, father molded pots, and my mother and I painted them in bright colors. Sometimes I was able to take walks, although they rarely let me go behind the city wall.'
$family_description['merchant'] = 'My father was a merchant and led caravans to distant countries. Me and my sisters often received different wonderful goodies, especially if he was leaving for a long time. We lived better than many of the townspeople, and, of course, better than the peasants in the villages.'
$family_description['valetry'] = 'My mother was a servant in the knight’s castle, and I never knew my father. It is possible that even the old lord didn’t know him, though I do not remember him much either. From early childhood I was taught to help and serve, but I also had a lot of time for games.'
$family_description['knight'] = 'I grew up in the castle of my father, together with my sisters and brothers. My father was absent for long periods of time as he went on military campaigns.'
$family_description['mprincess'] = 'From childhood on I was accustomed to luxury as a worthy princess. Although I was the youngest daughter, I was the most beloved. Mom and dad doted on me, and everyone in the castle executed my whims. Together with my sisters and the servants, we often played in the garden.'

$family_description['farmers'] = 'My family had a farm of about twenty acres. We cultivated corn, beans, and had a decent herd of cows. Since childhood I have helped my parents on the farm, and in my spare time played with neighborhood children in the nearby forest.'
$family_description['workhouse'] = 'My parents died when I was young, and under the law of the homeless I was assigned to be raised in a workhouse. We lived like in a prison, working from sunrise to sunset on the looms. If someone is not doing his rate, he is flogged.'
$family_description['proletarian'] = 'I was born to a working class family. Father worked at a steel mill, and mother at a textile factory. They work twelve hours per day and are very tired, so I had to keep the house and care for my sick grandmother.'

$family_description['ingeneer'] = 'I was born to the family of an engineer. Father maintained and repaired boilers and other units for the nearest factory. This work is very important, because without machines the whole factory will stop working.'

$family_description['buissinesman'] = 'I grew up in a fairly wealthy family. Father owned an office in wholesale trade of spare parts, and my mother was a homemaker. And we also had a housekeeper. $family_description['finance'] = 'My father was a tough stockbroker, and my mother an actress in the theater. However, when I grew up, she no longer worked. Dad spent little time at home. Mom suspected him of infidelity and drank a lot, then became addicted to painkillers. Sometimes she would get angry at me, so I also did not like to stay at home.'
$family_description['general'] = 'My father was a general, and he kept strict order in the family. I think he wanted me to be a boy, then he could force me to march and do other stupid things. Although we were financially independent, I was jealous of the other children, who didn’t have such harsh rules at home.'

$family_description['poet'] = 'My parents had a unique sense of language. My mother was a structural linguist, and my father was a poet, and very famous besides. We had a rule in the house that we were allowed to talk only in verse, and they taught me to do so as soon as I began to speak.'
$family_description['artist'] = 'My mother was a great artist. Her talent was recognized all over the world. She, of course, gladly shared her secrets with the younger artists and held a course of color expression at the open university. I inherited my love for drawing from her.'
$family_description['architect'] = 'My parents were architects and always worked as a pair. $family_description['operator'] = 'My mother worked as a production operator in the polar replication center. I did not have a father, and the far north is not the best place for a child. Therefore, I was brought up in a public childcare center, and I came to visit my mother only on weekends.'

$family_description['jailer'] = 'I was born and grew up in a giant prison complex. My father worked there as a security guard, so according to law our housing was provided at his workplace. Our free state has a lot of domestic enemies, and because of that it needs big prisons.'
$family_description['bioreactor'] = 'I grew up in the underground complex where my parents worked. They maintained a bioreactor that turned our enemies and other dregs of society into valuable fertilizer.
